# Script Index

## Generated-Root WBP t184 Root-First Feasibility Gate - 2026-07-03

| Path | Purpose | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12RootFirstFeasibilityGateV0.py --preset default\|expanded` | Read-only root-first dual-axis feasibility gate prototype | Normalizes existing root/reservation/product-probe reports into `PASS/BORDERLINE/FAIL`, soft `capacityScore`, `routingDecision`, and `probeOutcome`. Default t184a cases are c027-like capacity reference, t182 boundary-owned root family, c038 micro capacity control, and root154 cross-basin control. Expanded t184b adds dirty-required c038/c043, frame-mismatch root10, and c043 stage control. It does not generate levels and must not feed `probeCollapse` back into the hard compatibility gate. |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12LimitedUDGProbePlannerV0.py` | Read-only planner for t184 gray-zone limited UDG probes | Reads the t184b gate CSV and emits t184c probe plan rows/commands. It verifies `baseCsv/baseLevelId/seedstatePlanCsv`, target seed-chain count, and existing evidence. Default budget is readiness-sized (`micro1x1`, `seedGroups1`, `raw20`, `beam1`, `greedy7/10`) and must not be treated as a full capacity run. |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12LimitedUDGProbeResultAuditV0.py` | Read-only audit for executed t184 limited UDG probe outputs | Reads the t184c plan and classifies actual output as `coverageProbePass`, `coverageProbeNoBundle`, `seedOnlyEntryPassCoverageProbeUnavailable`, or `notExecutedGateReject`. It calibrates gray-zone routing only; it does not rewrite the hard compatibility gate. |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12RootFamilyCapacityPreflightV0.py` | Read-only t185 root-family capacity/wave-shape preflight | Joins t184b/t184c/t184d with historical candidate evidence and classifies each family as `MicroWaveRunnable`, `BatchFirstRequired`, `SeedEntryOnlyOfflineCoverage`, or `RejectedByCompatibility`. It selects the next UDG search shape per root family and does not generate levels. |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12WaveShapeAwareRoutePlannerV0.py` | Read-only t185b wave-shape-aware UDG route planner | Consumes t185a and t184c to emit calibrated commands per root family: c038/c043 no-dirty narrow micro sweeps, root154 batch-first `12,4,4,1`, and t182 offline/tailored dirty-owned capacity. |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12WaveShapeRouteExecutionAuditV0.py` | Read-only t185c execution audit for t185b route outputs | Reads already-written t185b outputs and classifies current-code replay as `CurrentReplayHasRows`, `HistoricalReplayDiverged`, `OfflineRouteNotExecuted`, `CurrentMicroSweepNoRows`, or `NotRunByPlan`. Use it to avoid confusing materializer replay drift with root compatibility. |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12WaveShapeReplayDriftDiffV0.py` | Read-only t185d historical-vs-current wave replay diff | Joins t185a/t185b/t185c and compares historical wave audits against current replay wave audits. It identifies first divergence wave, max historical/current wave, bundle-count drift, and whether the issue is replay truncation rather than root compatibility. |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12Wave1HistoricalOptionReplayAuditV0.py` | Read-only t185e wave-1 option replay audit | Matches historical wave-1 cells against current option audit outputs. Important: `BCLxxxxx` ids are enumeration-local labels and must not be used as stable identity across runs. |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12SelectorCalibrationAuditV0.py` | Read-only t185h selector calibration summary | Summarizes t185f/t185g selector probes and classifies `PassOptionsVisibleButNotSelected`, `Wave1Recovered`, `HistoricalWindowRecovered`, and `InteractiveTimeoutNoOutput`. Use after replay probes to distinguish root failure from selector visibility/gate drift. |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12UnifiedDutyGraphMultiWaveCoverageV1.py --require-single-coverage-greedy-solved` | Calibrated replay input-domain gate for t185 | For root154, this restores the historical full `12,4,4,1` capacity window to `0.8684211`. Use as a replay/calibration control before comparing root-family capacity; do not silently apply it as a product difficulty proof. |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12CalibratedRoutePlannerV1.py` | Read-only t186 calibrated route planner | Consumes t185a/t185b/t185h and emits calibrated next commands. Hard compatibility rejects stay skipped; root154 is interactive batch replay with `--require-single-coverage-greedy-solved`; c038/c043 are offline segmented micro replay; t182 is dirty-owned offline capacity. |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12SegmentedMicroReplayPlannerV1.py` | Read-only t186b segmented micro replay planner | Expands t186a c038/c043 `prepare_segmented_micro_replay` rows into prefix-from-root commands for micro `1,2,4,6,8,12,16,20,24`. These are capacity-curve probes, not true resume chunks, because UDG reloads the original `rootPath` for each run. |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-GeneratedRootWBPV12SegmentedMicroReplayResultAuditV1.py` | Read-only t186c segmented replay result audit | Reads the t186b plan and classifies each prefix as `RanWithCandidates`, `RanNoCandidates`, `PlannedNotRun`, or `NotRunnable`, then reports best coverage/Greedy/release-domain curve by case. |

路径以仓库根目录为基准。先按用途找入口，再读取具体脚本和相邻实现。

## Runtime

| Path | 用途 | 什么时候看 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `Assets/ArrowMagic/Scripts/Board/` | 棋盘、tile、链条和玩法核心 | 修改棋盘行为、消除逻辑、坐标/网格规则 |
| `Assets/ArrowMagic/Scripts/Generation/ArrowLevelGeneratorAdapter.cs` | package DTO 与项目资产之间的生成适配 | 接入 `com.pixelbug.arrow-level-generator` 或转换关卡数据 |
| `Assets/ArrowMagic/Scripts/IO/LevelIO.cs` | 关卡 IO 基础入口 | 读写关卡数据、排查序列化 |
| `Assets/ArrowMagic/Scripts/IO/LevelLoader.cs` | 关卡加载 | 场景加载关卡、包引用、启动关卡 |
| `Assets/ArrowMagic/Scripts/IO/LevelProgression.cs` | 关卡进度 | 关卡顺序、解锁、进度保存相关任务 |
| `Assets/ArrowMagic/Scripts/IO/LevelSaveData.cs` | 存档数据结构 | 修改存档字段、迁移进度数据 |
| `Assets/ArrowMagic/Scripts/UI/ArrowMagicHudUIITK.cs` | UI Toolkit HUD 控制 | 修改游戏 HUD、按钮、状态显示 |
| `Assets/ArrowMagic/Scripts/UI/UIToolkitTileRenderer.cs` | UI Toolkit tile 渲染 | 修改 tile 外观、棋盘视觉映射 |
| `Assets/ArrowMagic/Scripts/ScriptableObjects/` | LevelDefinition、LevelPack 等 SO 类型 | 改关卡/包数据结构时先看 |

| --- | --- | --- |

| `.worktrees/sgp-building-grammar/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-PressureReadStageLockVariants.ps1` | Building Grammar CPS/interleave StageLock 实验 | 当前分支支持 `-OutputPrefix`、`-SourceSortMode CrossPotential`、`-InterleavedLockBias`、`-MinCrossPotentialScore`、`-CrossPotentialOnly`、`interleaveSolveHead/availableTraceHead` 调试字段和 interleave-aware dependency merge guard；`InterleaveFlipPasses` 默认 0，pair-flip/`-EnableInterleaveDominanceTrim` 仅显式实验；新增 `-UltraChoiceEvalLimit` 防止坏源在 ultra prune 中拖到外部超时，`-AllowTightCurveStageException` 仅用于紧选择曲线但 stage 分层略弱的显式 probe；`-EnableCurveRootStraightPrune`、`-EnableTightRootPairSearch`、`-EnableFollowRunStraightCut`、`-EnableSoftInterleaveDominanceTrim` 都是显式 probe 开关，目前不能作为默认量产参数；soft trim 已加 stage/curve/interleave floors，只能视为安全修复通道，不代表已能 strict 量产；2026-06-21 新增 scheduled trace/weak sidecar diagnostics 和失衡 cross flip 拒绝，结论是后验 flip 可造伪 cross 但不能稳定突破 dual-spine；v175 证明 `-StageGateSearch -UltraLowChoiceBias` 能把 h231 类高结构源压成低选择 near-pass；v176 进一步证明 top8 h231-like 源经该组合后可通过 stage-preserving pair repair 达到 `followRun=2/stage>=0.82`，下一步应自动化该 lane 而非继续 sidecar/trim |

| `.worktrees/sgp-building-grammar/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-StageLockSourceEnhancedVariants.ps1` | Building Grammar StageDoor 源增强实验 | 当前分支从 rhythm-lab 源增强脚本派生，支持 `StageDoorProfile=DualBalanced` 与 `DualCarrier` 实验；`DualCarrier` 会输出 `dualCarrierBridgeCount/dualCarrierMergeCounts` 并禁用普通 fallback，用于诊断双 carrier/跨侧 bridge 是否真实形成。当前结论：能造出 `cross≈0.048` 的早期信号，但仍会在 choice curve 与真实双线之间拉扯，不能作为 dual-spine 量产突破 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-building-grammar/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-DependencyAnchorSourceVariants.ps1` | Building Grammar dependency anchor 源注入 | 从自然高覆盖 SGP/StageLock 成品出发，解析 `LevelDefinition` 并选择少量 target/blocker 逃逸射线依赖候选，只翻转 target 链来注入 dependency anchor；支持 `-UseFinalPath` 直接锚定最终 curated body，也支持 `-EnableInterruptorSidecar` 做 source-side sidecar 实验。v163-v166 结论：final-body h91 可到 relaxed pass 且 strict 仅差 `followRun=3`，但单纯提高 `anchorCrossCount` 会打开选择曲线；v172-v173 结论：source-side free sidecar 会提高选择数/破坏 realized cross，不作为主线；下一步应找 h231-like 可低选择门锁化源，并把 anti-follow 约束前移 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-building-grammar/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-DependencyFollowRunReport.ps1` | Building Grammar realized follow-run 诊断与 pair/triple/interruptor repair probe | 从最终 `LevelDefinition` 重算 greedy dependency follow-run，输出 max-run segment、逐步替代链、single/pair/triple flip probe；支持 `-ExportBestPairFlipRepair` / `-ExportAllPairFlipRepairs` / `-ExportAllTripleFlipRepairs` 导出 repair 资产；v171 新增 `-EnableInterruptorMergeProbe` / `-ExportAllInterruptorMergeRepairs` 和 `interruptorAltCount/CloseAlt/BestDeficit` 诊断；v197 修复 repair 导出长路径问题，并新增 `-ExportAllSingleFlipRepairs`、`-RepairAllowNoFollowGain`、`-RepairMinOpeners`、`-IncludeAllFlipCandidates`，用于 two-stage repair 中把 cross-preserving 冷候选拉回 `openers>=4` |

| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-PinDebtSGPFillProbeV1.ps1` | Pin-debt C+P 成对 probe | 2026-06-25 新增；从已验证小画布父本生成同一 SGP-style 候选链 `C` 的 `cOnly` 与 `cPin` 两个资产，`cPin` 会沿 `C` 的 direct ray 自动生成一条物理 Pin 链。用于验证“新外逃是否应该即时补钉子”。首轮 strict smoke 证明 Pin 会降低 choices/openers，但若不做 core/release gate 会高概率剪断 support closure，因此该脚本是诊断入口，不是生产填肉器。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-PinFieldRoleMapV2.ps1` | PinField role-map 编译 probe | 2026-06-25 新增；把 RayConstraintMap cells 转成 SGP adapter 可读的 role-map，尝试用整张约束场替代单链 Pin 验证。首轮 small-canvas probe 证明当前 cell-level field 两端都失败：hard pre-action field 会压低 outer/choice 但破可解和 support，soft field 能填但 outer/choice 爆；该脚本用于记录负例和后续 temporal release-lane field 对照。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-LaneConstraintFieldV0.ps1` | Release-lane 投影与 shuffle test | 2026-06-25 新增；从 RayConstraintMap edges/cells 抽 top direct critical lanes，输出 lanes CSV、soft role-map、hard reserve edges 和 shuffled reserve edges。首轮 V0 证明 head-only lane reserve 与 shuffled reserve 结果几乎相同，说明当前实现只是在减少 head 空间，没有编码真实 release-lane 语义。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-TraceBoundSGPProbeV0.ps1` | Trace-bound / trace-edge SGP candidate-language probe | 2026-06-25 新增；让 SGP-style 新链 head ray 绑定 trace 语义。V0 first-hit owner 绑定证明只撞同一 owner 不够；V1 `-UseTraceEdgeContract` 改为把新链插入原 dependency edge ray corridor。支持 `MinHitWave/MaxReleaseGap/MaxHitsPerEdge/ProtectCriticalRayBodyCells`。V1e 新增 `EdgeSchedulePreset=WaveBridgeV1`、`SkipFailedScheduledEdges`、`AvoidCriticalRayBodyCells`：当前最佳 smoke 12 个里 10 个 solved/S-A/supportDepth=4、outer=0，但平均只加 2.58 条，说明 trace-semantic scheduling 成立但 candidate throughput 仍不足。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Select-MigrationAwareTraceCandidatesV1.ps1` | Migration-aware trace candidate selector | 2026-06-25 新增；合并候选 CSV 与 board trace，把候选分类为 `SupportPreserved`、`HardMotifMigrated`、`SupportRootMigrated` 或 `Reject`。用于验证“允许难度骨架迁移”是否真的救出新 hard motif，而不是单纯放宽 supportDepth。首轮 trace-edge 批次只选出 SupportPreserved，没有发现 HardMotifMigrated。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-WavePeelRerootProbeV1.ps1` | Wave0 peel / re-root probe | 2026-06-25 新增；计算当前初始可消 wave/opener，默认保护 `baseChains` 父本骨架和 trace supportClosure owners，只处理后补出来的 opener 层。支持 `ReverseEligibleExceptKeep`（已证明会剪断释放顺序，作为负例）和 `DropEligibleExceptKeep`（有效把 SGP 爆选择层剥掉）。首轮 c05 中间态从 coverage `0.4808`/Drop 通过 drop 非骨架 opener 拉回 A，但覆盖回落；再次 SGP 可推到 `0.56` 后又 Drop，再次 peel 又回 A。该脚本证明“SGP 生成的是可剥 opener wave”，下一步要把 drop 空区替换成 root/gate refill，而不是留空。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-WavePeelReleaseScaffoldGroupV0.ps1` | Peeled-space release scaffold group probe | 2026-06-25 新增；从 SGP full source 与 peel 后 base 做 cell diff，只允许在被 peel 掉的非骨架空间里生成短链，且新链 head 必须 first-hit 到受保护 skeleton owner。用于验证“剥掉 opener wave 后把空区重编成 root/gate scaffold”是否比 trace-edge micro-fill 吞吐更高。首轮 k4 probe 可两轮推到 A/supportDepth=4 coverage `0.3923`，再往上会变 B/Drop。2026-06-25 追加 `-UsePeeledSourceChainSlots` / `-FallbackToAllPeeledCells` / `-MaxChainsPerSourceSlot`：按被 peel 的原 SGP source chain 分槽 refill，立即 pass 率提升到 19/32 A+supportDepth4，但再交给 raw SGP 仍会回到 Drop/outer 爆炸。追加实验参数 `-IncludeBoundaryMouthCells` / `-AllowBoundaryBodyCells` / `-RequireMouthCellHit` 用于 mouth-aware 堵口 probe；硬 mouth-hit 条件过紧，当前不作为默认。最新正信号来自“小步 SGP + 针对新增槽位 refill”：SGP 每次只加 2 根 direct-exit opener，再用 source-slot refill 重写这 2 根，可保持 solved/supportDepth4 并继续推进。2026-06-25 又新增 `-PeeledSlotHaloRadius`，用于高覆盖时给被剥 source slot 周围增加施工空间；halo2 可补满短槽位但当前会破 support/solvability，需配合 support-closure-aware owner/halo gate，不能单独作为生产默认。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-ReverseSlotRefillV1.py` | SGP slot 内 reverse-valid refill | 2026-06-25 新增；从 0.30 父本与一个 SGP full state 做 cell diff，把 SGP 新增格当作 slot，按 reverse solve order 在 slot 内生成可释放短链，并可输出 Unity `LevelDefinition` + candidate CSV。用于替代旧随机 owner-hit scaffold：它先保证新增链在简化 greedy/reverse 模型中可释放，再交给 `Build-SGPRhythmTrace.ps1` 验证。首轮 smoke 在 SGP `0.425` slot 内加 3 链，正式 trace 为 solved/A，openers `3`、avg/max `3.28/6`、supportDepth `4`，证明“SGP 找施工区 + reverse 补阻挡”成立；已支持 `--unity-top-k` 输出多资产候选。2026-06-26 增加 `--max-after-choices` 生成期选择数硬 cap 与 `--slot-ray-density-max` slot ray-density 过滤，用于 bulk reverse / neutral slot 实验。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-ReverseSandwichProductionLineV0.ps1` | Reverse Sandwich 正式生产线入口 | 2026-06-25 新增；串联 0.30 hard 父本、bounded SGP burst、growth-order 诊断、剥掉整批 SGP 新增 slot、`ReverseSlotRefillV1` 重填、最终 trace 和 final growth report。默认 `RefillMode=ReverseSlotRefillV1`，保留 `ReleaseScaffoldGroupV0` 作为负例/对照。用于验证用户提出的“SGP 先指定区域补；难度崩就拿掉 SGP 新增链；reverse 增加难度和阻挡”的正式闭环。2026-06-26 增加 `ReverseSeedBatches/ReverseSeedStride`；seed sweep 已能自动选中 solved/A/supportDepth4 reverse 候选。当前边界：小步稳定但吞吐低，大 SGP slot + bulk reverse 到 `0.62-0.65` 仍可解/support4 但 process Drop，距离 `0.9` 需要新的 ray-aware thinning / release-safe SGP 约束层。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-TailExtensionFillV1.py` | Existing-chain tail extension density fill | 2026-06-26 新增；只延长已有链尾，不新增 chain head，用于提高 coverage 而尽量不增加 opener。支持 `--max-choices` 和 `--max-blocker-value`。中性尾巴（不进入任何当前 ray）从 `0.499` 推到 `0.598`，正式 trace 为 solved/B/support3/openers10/avg3.87；ray-touching 尾巴可到 `0.865` 但全部 unsolved/support0，因此当前定位是 density filler/诊断，不是单独成品方案。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-sandwich-refill/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-FailurePocketExtractorV1.ps1` | Sandwich failure-pocket anchor extractor | 2026-06-25 clean worktree 新增；读取 `Build-SGPGrowthOrderReportV1.ps1` 的 growth CSV，抽取新增链 owner、first-hit owner、direct-exit opener，并输出下一轮 `FailurePocketAnchorMode/Owners` 命令片段。用于把手动 anchor 扩张升级为 failure-pocket scheduler。 |

| `.worktrees/sgp-sandwich-refill/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Invoke-FailurePocketSchedulerV1.ps1` | failure-pocket scheduler wrapper | 2026-06-25 clean worktree 新增；自动串联 Reward SGP、growth report、direct-exit pocket 选择、fast rewrite 和 trace accept。2026-06-26 追加多 Reward/多单口尝试、B-tier debt 接受门槛、可配置 rewrite 长度、真实 committed owner anchor，以及 `-AllowRewardDebtCommit` 允许 Reward 本身在 solved/supportDepth4 且 A/S/B 债务阈值内直接 commit。最新 sandwich 边界：可稳定到约 `0.6846 B/supportDepth4`；之后 SGP one-chain 候选坍缩为固定 owner-hit，supportDepth 掉到 2，现有 fast rewrite len10 仍救不回 support4。 |

| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-SeededDirectSGPFillBaselineV1.ps1` | Seeded Direct-SGP 满铺/小画布基线 | 2026-06-24 新增；把 package `DirectRectangleArrowLevelGenerator` 的 layer-head/inward-growth/family scoring/remaining heads 思路改成“以已验证 0.30 父本为已占用格”的 seeded fill baseline，并可选 `-EnableMicroFill` 模拟 shape-heal/micro-fill。已修复 `paths:` vs `authoredLevel.arrows:` 写入 bug；修正版证明 0.30 父本无约束可几何满铺到 coverage `0.9436-0.9510`，但 trace 全部 Drop、choices/outer 爆炸。2026-06-24 扩展 `CanvasWidth/CanvasHeight/MaxTotalChains` 用于小画布验证；当前最小不坏画布为 18x24。`PreseedOuterFrame` + `MinHeadLayer=1` 是当前有效路线：先铺外围短框架再让 SGP 内填，18x24/max44 可得到 4 个 supportDepth=3 的 solved/A review 样本，coverage `0.5602-0.6134`。2026-06-24 又扩展 Constraint Adapter / `UsePreActionMask`：软预算 adapter 可恢复高 coverage 但无法阻止 outer-exit collapse；pre-action mask 可显著降低外口但单独会 early deadlock。新增 `PreActionMaskAllowReleaseHeads`/`PreActionMaskReleaseRegions` 证明“放开 critical/release-region head”仍只到约 0.6 且 unsolved；结论：该脚本可继续作为 SGP 行为对照和 release-scaffold 实验底座，不应继续只调 adapter/head 白名单。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-SeededDirectSGPFillBaselineV1.ps1` | Full-ray release-lane reserve probe | 2026-06-24 扩展 `PreActionMaskReserveFullRayOwners`，可把指定 parent owner 从 head 到边界的完整逃逸射线加入 adapter reserved cells；同时修复 `Try-BuildChain` 第二格未走 adapter step rejection 的漏洞。实测只保留 `rayCellsBeforeHit` 会继续断 temporal release；full-ray 最小 closure 可恢复 solved/supportDepth=4，但 coverage 约 `0.45-0.47`，说明 full release lane 是正确 scaffold，下一步要从“禁区”升级为 temporal-aware controlled lane。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-SeededDirectSGPFillBaselineV1.ps1` | SGP LDF / block-relation head scoring | 2026-06-25 扩展 `-UseLocalDifficultyField`、`-EmitLdfHeadReport` 和 `-UseLdfSupplementalBlockerHeads`。LDF V1 对现有 outward heads 按 direct-exit、first-hit owner 和 escape-ray blocker reward 打分；可用 `*_ldf_head_report.csv` 审计候选语言。实测 outward-only LDF 可小幅降低 choices/outer 且保 solved/support，但仍 Drop；补充 non-direct blocker heads 可强压 choices/outer 但无 release-wave 调度会 `0/4` solved、supportDepth=0。用于诊断/下一代 release-scheduled head provider，不是生产默认。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-SeededDirectSGPFillBaselineV1.ps1` | SGP release-aware head provider V2 probe | 2026-06-25 扩展 `-UseReleaseAwareHeadProviderV2`、`-ReleaseAwareEdgesCsv`、release wave/gap/head cap 和 `-ReleaseAwareAvoidCriticalRayBodyCells`。V2 从 `criticalDependencyEdge` 的 ray cells 提供非 direct head，并要求当前 first-hit 回原 edge owner/wave。A/B 证明它能比 LDF 更强压 choices/outer 且保 solved，但 head-only 会导致 supportDepth drift；下一步应升级为 body/corridor-bound release contract，而不是继续调 head reward/cap。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-SeededDirectSGPFillBaselineV1.ps1` | SGP head+body corridor contract V1 | 2026-06-25 扩展 `ReleaseAwareBodyCorridorSteps/Distance/Reward/Penalty`，只对 `releaseAwareV2` head 的前 N 步 body 加 corridor soft bias。2-head forced run 保持 `4/4 solved/supportDepth=4` 并降低 avg/max/outer；4-head run supportDepth 全掉到 2。当前安全基线是 2 条 corridor-bound release heads；下一步需要 per-owner/per-wave budget，不应盲目加 head 数。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-SeededDirectSGPFillBaselineV1.ps1` | SGP release-aware budget/wave-window scheduler V1 | 2026-06-25 扩展 `ReleaseAwareAcceptedPerOwnerBudget`、`ReleaseAwareAcceptedPerHitOwnerBudget`、`ReleaseAwareAcceptedPerHitWaveBudget`、`ReleaseAwareAcceptedPerOwnerWaveBudget`、`ReleaseAwareAcceptedPerEdgeBudget`、`ReleaseAwareAcceptedTotalBudget`、`ReleaseAwareMaxHitWave`、`ReleaseAwareMaxOwnerWave`。实验结论：exact owner/wave dedup 不能救 4-head collapse；`ReleaseAwareMaxHitWave=3` 才复现安全 `4/4 solved/supportDepth=4`。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-SeededDirectSGPFillBaselineV1.ps1` | SGP Stage-2 emission / grammar probes | 2026-06-25 扩展 `UsePostKernelEmissionController` 与 `PostKernel*` scoring 参数；activation 后会重启同层 head 排序，让 Stage-2 scoring 真正作用于后续 native heads。随后新增 `UsePostKernelCandidateAugmentor`、`PostKernelAugmentor*` 和 `PostKernelRecomputeAfterChain`，提供非直出 first-hit-owner post-kernel heads并可在 commit 后刷新 LDF/BlockMap。0.55 augmentor probe 保住 `4/4 solved/supportDepth=4`，但非直出 head 数量太少，native direct-exit 仍主导。2026-06-25 追加 `UsePostKernelGrammarUnits`、`PostKernelGrammar*` 和 `fixedPrefixCells`，用于 SGP-3L Stage2 mini-chain grammar probe；V0 可大幅降低 direct/outer/choice，但 `0/4 solved`，说明 generic mini-chain grammar 会剪断 spine。2026-06-25 追加 `UsePostKernelTraceEdgeGrammarUnits`、`PostKernelTraceEdgeGrammar*`、trace-edge commit reachability check 和 local edge relay support proxy；edge-corridor grammar 有吞吐并可恢复 solved，但 reachability/local-edge proxy 仍会降 supportDepth。2026-06-25 继续追加 `PostKernelTraceEdgeGrammarUseClosureShadow`、`PostKernelTraceEdgeGrammarClosureDepth`、`PostKernelTraceEdgeGrammarMinShadowRatio`：support-root closure shadow 可保 `supportDepth=4`，但当前吞吐过低且 broad-window 太慢，因此定位为 safety gate/诊断，不是最终 Stage2 pressure language。2026-06-25 追加 `PostKernelTraceEdgeGrammarUseClosureCompatiblePrefilter`、`PostKernelTraceEdgeGrammarBasinDepth/Distance/MaxAffectedRoots`：可把 TraceEdge prefix/body 限制到 closure basin envelope；窄域 prefilter 会真实改变候选空间，但仍不能单独保证 supportDepth，应用作下一代 support-depth-preserving grammar/top-K direct check 的输入。2026-06-25 追加 `PostKernelTraceEdgeGrammarUseWitnessGate` 与 witness edge survival 参数；TraceEdge-only witness exact/relay 未触发拒绝，说明当前 support 漏洞主要来自后续 native post-kernel direct chains。2026-06-25 追加 native direct commit probes：`UsePostKernelNativeSupportPressureBudget`、`UsePostKernelNativeDirectIdentityGate`、`UsePostKernelNativeSupportShadowGate`。SPB/identity/shadow 三者均为负向边界：分别证明 scalar budget、bad-anchor reuse 和当前 support-root shadow proxy 不能修复 native direct support leak。 |
| `.worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-OwnerHitGrammarFillV1.py` | SGP sandwich support-safe owner-hit grammar fill / geometry supply owner-hit probe | 2026-06-26 新增；从当前父本空格枚举非直出、first-hit 旧骨架 owner 的小链候选，按贪心不过峰、blocker value、hit distance、hit owner 多样性预筛后输出候选 CSV，最终仍交给 `Build-SGPRhythmTrace.ps1` 做提交真值。支持 opt-in `--supply-level`、`--supply-fit exact|center-crop`、`--supply-require-edges`，用于把普通 PressureHard/PSG 样本只当几何/同链边供料，不继承其 LocalEasy 难度判断。支持 opt-in bundle 模式：`--bundle-count`、`--bundle-pool-count`、`--bundle-same-hit-cap`、`--bundle-require-old-hit`，一次候选放多条不重叠且最终 first-hit 老骨架 owner 的供料链，用于提高吞吐。当前 best：root10+dense_weave+bundle3 到 `0.5000/A/TrueHardCandidate/supportDepth4`；root05+core_burst 到 `0.6419/S/MediumStructure/supportDepth4`。 |

| Path | 用途 | 什么时候看 |

## Root Family Classifiers / Generators - 2026-06-24 09:24 additions

- .worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-SplitKeyRootClassifierV1.ps1 - classifies split-key root candidates using three-lock core ray, anti-dual, anti-cascade and low-fanout checks.
- .worktrees/sgp-rhythm-lab/Tools/SGPRhythmLab/Build-RootTopologyTemplateGeneratorV1.ps1 - now includes split_key_dependency template in addition to existing root primitives.
